			value = 0

		set_variable = {

			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = target_distance
			value = 0
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			variable_name = target_trust
			value = trust
			who = FROM
			with = ROOT
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = target_trust
			value = 50
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = target_trust
			value = 2
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			variable_name = target_opinion
			value = opinion
			who = FROM
			with = ROOT
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = target_opinion
			value = 0.1
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			variable_name = target_dip_rep
			value = modifier:diplomatic_reputation
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = target_dip_rep
			value = -2
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			variable_name = sender_dip_rep
			value = modifier:diplomatic_reputation
			who = FROM
		}
		multiply_variable = {

			value = 2
		}

			which = target_distance
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = ai_likelyhood
			which = ai_value
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = ai_likelyhood
			value = 100
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = ai_likelyhood
			value = 0.5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of_type = appanage_subject
				FROM = {
					tag = FRA
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = edit_de_moulins
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_likelyhood
				value = 0.01
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ai_likelyhood
						value = 0.01
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_likelyhood
				value = 0.01
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ai_likelyhood
					value = 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_likelyhood
				value = 100
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = bonding_tributary
		}
		country_event = {
			id = diplomacy_events.002
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = diplomacy_events.003
	title = "diplomacy_events.003.name"
	desc = "diplomacy_events.003.desc"
	picture = OVERLORDVASSAL_eventPicture

		name = "diplomacy_events.003.opta"
		FROM = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = close_tributary_state
				subject = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = diplomacy_events.004
	title = "diplomacy_events.004.name"

	option = {
		name = "diplomacy_events.004.opta"
		add_ruler_modifier = {

			duration = -1
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = diplomacy_events.011
	title = "diplomacy_events.011.name"
	desc = "diplomacy_events.011.desc"
	picture = POLICY_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = "diplomacy_events.011.opta"
		random_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = policy_partner
				}
				NOT = {
					liberty_desire = 25
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_subject_of_type = vassal
						years_in_vassalage_under = {
							who = ROOT
							years = 10
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_subject_of_type = personal_union
						years_in_union_under = {
							who = ROOT
							years = 10
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = subject_01

				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = subject_20
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = subject_01
			save_event_target_as = target_subject_01
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = target_trust

			}
			set_variable = {
				which = sender_legitimacy
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = target_reptrad
				value = 0

					which = Assimilation_Process
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = Remaining_Years
					which = Assimilation_Process
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = Remaining_Years
					which = Years_as_Vassal
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						overlord = {
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								NOT = {
									is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								}
								NOT = {
									is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = overlord_subject
							}
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							overlord_of = PREV
						}
						country_event = {
							id = subject_integration.201
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = overlord_subject
					}
					clr_country_flag = overlord_subject
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = Integration_Factor
					which = Years_as_Vassal
				}
				multiply_variable = {
					which = Integration_Factor
					value = 100
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = Assimilation_Process
							value = 0
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					divide_variable = {
						which = Integration_Factor
						which = Assimilation_Process
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = diplomacy_events.012
		}
	}

								value = 1.65
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.70
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.70
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.75
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.75
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.80
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.80
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.85
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.85
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.90
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.90
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.95
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.95
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 2.00
							}
						}
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = {
					which = Assimilation_Process
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = Remaining_Years
					which = Assimilation_Process
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = Remaining_Years
					which = Years_as_Vassal
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						overlord = {
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								NOT = {
									is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								}
								NOT = {
									is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = overlord_subject
							}
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							overlord_of = PREV
						}
						country_event = {
							id = subject_integration.201
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = overlord_subject
					}
					clr_country_flag = overlord_subject
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = Integration_Factor
					which = Years_as_Vassal
				}
				multiply_variable = {
					which = Integration_Factor
					value = 100
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = Assimilation_Process
							value = 0
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					divide_variable = {
						which = Integration_Factor
						which = Assimilation_Process
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = diplomacy_events.022
		}
	}
}

								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.90
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.90
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_modifier_value = {
								which = diplomatic_annexation_cost
								value = -0.95
							}
						}
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 1.95
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						PREV = {
							divide_variable = {
								which = Assimilation_Process
								value = 2.00
							}
						}
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = {
					which = Assimilation_Process
					value = 10
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = Remaining_Years
					which = Assimilation_Process
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = Remaining_Years
					which = Years_as_Vassal
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						overlord = {
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								NOT = {
									is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								}
								NOT = {
									is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = overlord_subject
							}
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							overlord_of = PREV
						}
						country_event = {
							id = subject_integration.201
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = overlord_subject
					}
					clr_country_flag = overlord_subject
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = Integration_Factor
					which = Years_as_Vassal
				}
				multiply_variable = {
					which = Integration_Factor
					value = 100
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = Assimilation_Process
							value = 0
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					divide_variable = {
						which = Integration_Factor
						which = Assimilation_Process
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = diplomacy_events.032
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = diplomacy_events.035
	title = "diplomacy_events.035.name"
	desc = "diplomacy_events.035.desc"
	picture = OVERLORDVASSAL_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = "diplomacy_events.035.opta"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = appanage_subject
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = autonomous_vassal
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = decentralized_vassal
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = rebellious_decentralized_vassal
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = decentralized_vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = subjugated_vassal
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = rebellious_subjugated_vassal
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = subjugated_vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = daimyo_vassal
				}
				culture_group = japanese
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = centralised_daimyo_vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of_type = centralised_daimyo_vassal
				}
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = vassal
				subject = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = policy_partner
				hidden = yes
			}
			add_liberty_desire = 10
		}
	}
}

			which = ai_likelyhood
			value = 0.5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of_type = appanage_subject
				FROM = {
					tag = FRA
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = edit_de_moulins
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_likelyhood
				value = 0.01
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ai_likelyhood
						value = 0.01
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_likelyhood
				value = 0.01
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ai_likelyhood
					value = 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ai_likelyhood
				value = 100
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = subjugating_fief
		}
		country_event = {
			id = diplomacy_events.042
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
